### 1. 怀旧照片分析与重现（可口可乐男孩）

**Author**: [Heisenberg](https://x.com/rovvmut_)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用作图像分析请求，为一张怀旧的竖幅照片提供了大量的元数据和上下文。它描述了场景（小男孩靠在一台老式可口可乐自动售货机旁）、环境（刺眼的阳光、浓重的阴影）以及技术构图细节，很可能旨在指导 AI 高保真地重现或分析该图像。

![怀旧照片分析与重现（可口可乐男孩）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804273743_405m8w_G-7Jx2OXYAATnQw.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "image_quality": "Medium",
    "image_type": "Photo",
    "resolution_estimation": "Likely scanned from film, approx 1000x1500 effective detail",
    "file_characteristics": {
      "compression_artifacts": "Low",
      "noise_level": "Medium (Film grain present)",
      "lens_type_estimation": "Standard focal length (35mm or 50mm equivalent)"
    }
  },
  "global_context": {
    "scene_description": "A vertical, nostalgic photograph capturing a young boy leaning against a vintage Coca-Cola vending machine while drinking from a glass bottle. To the left is a dark, wooden cylindrical object (likely a barrel or trash receptacle). The scene is bathed in bright, harsh sunlight, creating strong shadows and high contrast. The setting appears to be an exterior alcove or storefront with visible conduits on the wall.",
    "environment_type": "Outdoor/Semi-outdoor storefront",
    "time_of_day": "Day (likely mid-day given the steep shadow angles)",
    "weather_atmosphere": "Clear, Sunny, Hot, Summer",
    "lighting": {
      "source": "Sunlight",
      "direction": "Top-left",
      "quality": "Hard, direct",
      "color_temperature": "Warm/Neutral"
    },
    "color_palette": {
      "dominant_hex_estimates": [
        "#D12E2E",
        "#EAEAEA",
        "#2A1A15",
        "#D6C6AA",
        "#4A3B32"
      ],
      "accent_colors": [
        "#008080",
        "#F4C430"
      ],
      "contrast_level": "High"
    }
  },
  "composition": {
    "camera_angle": "Eye-level with subject",
    "framing": "Full shot (knees up)",
    "depth_of_field": "Medium (background wall slightly soft but legible)",
    "focal_point": "Boy drinking soda",
    "symmetry_type": "None",
    "rule_of_thirds_alignment": "Boy aligns with left vertical third line; Machine aligns with right two-thirds"
  },
  "objects": [
    {
      "id": "obj_001",
      "label": "Young Boy",
      "category": "Person",
      "location": {
        "relative_position": "Center-left",
        "bounding_box_percentage": {
          "x": 0.25,
          "y": 0.38,
          "width": 0.35,
          "height": 0.58
        }
      },
      "dimensions_relative": "Medium",
      "distance_from_camera": "Mid",
      "pose_orientation": "Standing, leaning back, head tilted up drinking, legs crossed (left over right)",
      "material": "Organic/Textile",
      "surface_properties": {
        "texture": "Skin smooth, Fabric ribbed/wrinkled",
        "reflectivity": "Low",
        "micro_details": "Sunlit hair tips (halo effect), relaxed facial expression",
        "wear_state": "N/A"
      },
      "color_details": {
        "base_color_hex": "#F0D9C5",
        "secondary_colors": [
          "#FFFFFF",
          "#E8E8E8"
        ],
        "gradient_or_pattern": "Solid white clothing"
      },
      "interaction_with_light": {
        "shadow_casting": "Casts a sharp shadow onto the red vending machine behind him",
        "highlight_zo"
      }
```

**Author**: [Nurian](https://x.com/NeuralPaints)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度受限且详细的 JSON 提示，旨在生成一个类似于哈莉·奎茵（Harley Quinn）的图像，但没有明确提及她的名字。它使用严格模式和高保真度来定义“混乱的朋克魅力美学”，指定了独特的特征，例如异色瞳、特定的纹身（“ROTTEN”、心形），以及标志性的“Daddy's Lil Monster”T 恤和分色亮片热裤。

![哈莉·奎茵 原型图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804249243_ys4jjg_G-6yzh9WYAAha0p.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "priority": "High Fidelity",
    "strict_mode": true
  },
  "subject_core": {
    "visual_concept": "(Young woman with chaotic punk-glamour aesthetic:1.3)",
    "archetype": "Villainess, Anti-hero, (Manic expression:1.2)"
  },
  "appearance_strict": {
    "hair": "High pigtails, (platinum blonde roots:1.1), (dip-dyed bright pink left tip:1.4), (dip-dyed bright blue right tip:1.4), messy texture",
    "eyes": "((Heterochromia:1.5)), left eye electric blue, right eye emerald green, (heavy smudged eyeshadow:1.2)",
    "face_marks": "Pale porcelain skin, ((small black heart tattoo on cheekbone:1.5)), (('ROTTEN' text tattoo on jawline:1.4))",
    "expression": "Sly knowing smirk, wide smile, slightly manic energy"
  },
  "attire_strict": {
    "torso": "Torn white long-sleeve raglan shirt, text on chest reads (('Daddy's Lil Monster':1.5)), red neckline, visible black bra straps",
    "legs": "((Sequined hot pants:1.3)), split color design (left leg blue, right leg red), fishnet stockings",
    "feet": "High-top wedge sneakers, black and white, lace-up"
  },
  "props_strict": {
    "primary_weapon": "Wooden baseball bat held behind neck, large handwritten text on bat reads (('GOOD NIGHT':1.4))",
    "jewelry": "Thick gold spiked cuffs, (studded choker necklace:1.2)"
  },
  "environment": {
    "background": "Solid white studio background",
    "lighting": "High-key studio lighting, sharp focus, commercially lit"
  },
  "negative_constraints": [
    "generic cosplay",
    "low quality",
    "blurred text",
    "misspelled text",
    "wrong hair colors",
    "symmetrical eye color",
    "modest clothing",
    "dark background",
    "3d render",
```

```
Luxury brand about page, storytelling layout, 4:5 ratio.
```

### 15. 360 度等距柱状全景图提示

**Author**: [Aimi Kōda](https://x.com/aimikoda)  **Date**: 2026-01-18  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，旨在生成无缝的 360 度等距柱状全景图像，并针对整个球形视图中的一致光照和构图进行了优化。它指定了一个历史场景，并包含防止接缝或定向阴影等视觉伪影的规则，使其成为虚拟现实环境的理想选择。

![360 度等距柱状全景图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804204059_0knjxw_G-6FROjXwAAhlGv.jpg)
![360 度等距柱状全景图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804204223_htd648_G-6FhchXQAAg2v9.jpg)
![360 度等距柱状全景图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804204700_mp84c0_G-6FROdXEAA5Ebi.jpg)
![360 度等距柱状全景图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804205830_ybuinq_G-3jkdbWIAA-73-.jpg)
![360 度等距柱状全景图提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804205613_2j0lcg_G-3iiIrWsAEbmso.jpg)

```
[SCENE] = {argument name="scene description" default="Troy, Anatolia, approx. 12th century BC. The moments after the Trojan Horse is pulled inside the city walls."}

Make a 360-degree equirectangular panorama in 21:9 aspect ratio.
Render the scene as a full spherical panorama with correct equirectangular projection.
Set the entire environment strictly based on [SCENE].
Place the camera at the exact center of the scene with a fixed viewpoint.
Design the environment as a continuous, circular world with no left or right edge.
Ensure the first and last horizontal edges align perfectly.
Distribute architecture, people, and objects evenly around the full 360° view.
Use realistic real-world lighting, materials, and physical behavior.
Keep sharp focus across the entire panorama.
Use uniform natural daylight with no dominant light direction.
Ensure lighting intensity and color remain consistent across the full 360° panorama.
Treat the environment as lit by an evenly diffused sky dome rather than a single sun source.
Apply soft global shadows that do not favor any horizontal direction.
Avoid directional sunlight gradients that could cause seam lighting mismatches.
Avoid modern elements, UI overlays, borders, frames, cropped views, fantasy styling, or broken panorama seams.
```

**Author**: [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/iamdomprompt)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: en

> 一个超写实的提示词，用于生成一张高度风格化的美食艺术奇幻图像，画面中悉尼·斯威尼（Sydney Sweeney）装扮成埃及艳后，斜倚在一艘完全由果仁蜜饼雕塑而成的巨大驳船上，在蜂蜜之河中航行，背景是杏仁糖制成的金字塔。该提示词要求电影级灯光、极致细节和 16K 分辨率。

![悉尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 饰演的埃及艳后 (Cleopatra) 乘坐果仁蜜饼驳船 (Baklava Barge) 的美食艺术幻想](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717555657_39onnk_G-4v2yYWIAApQaa.jpg)

```
An ultra-photorealistic, highly stylized fine art photograph. {argument name="subject" default="Sydney Sweeney"}, styled dramatically as Cleopatra in ancient Egyptian gold and jewel-toned attire, is reclining languidly on a colossal, floating barge. The barge is a masterpiece of confectionary architecture, sculpted entirely from golden-brown, flaky baklava, dripping with clear sugar syrup and heavily dusted with edible 24k gold leaf and crushed pistachios.

The barge navigates vast, reflective rivers of thick, viscous dark amber honey, which casts deep, warm reflections. In the distance, massive, geometrically perfect pyramids rise, constructed entirely from textured, off-white marzipan, meticulously adorned with fine saffron threads and sesame seeds.

**Composition and Detail:** Low-angle wide shot, emphasizing the scale of the food architecture and the drama of the environment. Extreme attention to the textures: the sharp crispness of the baklava layers, the glossy sheen of the flowing honey, and the slightly granular, matte quality of the marzipan pyramids.

**Lighting and Atmosphere:** Cinematic studio lighting setup. Dominant warm, golden-hour fill lights emphasizing the opulence of the gold leaf and the deep amber tones of the honey. A powerful, focused rim light defines the edges of Cleopatra's form and highlights the flaky layers of the baklava barge. Subtle volumetric haze and golden dust motes float above the honey, creating a dreamy, luxurious atmosphere.

**Camera Settings:** Shot on Hasselblad X2D, 85mm lens, f/1.4. Highly detailed, cinematic aspect ratio (21:9), deep depth of field, 16K resolution, hyper-detailed food art photography.
---
```

### 49. 2x2 网格产品发明可视化（专利/营销）

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂的多面板提示，旨在通过结合两个概念（或演变其中一个）来可视化新产品的发明和营销。它要求采用 2x2 网格结构，每个象限都需要独特的视觉风格：技术线条艺术（爆炸专利视图）、示意图（功能图）、照片级真实感渲染图（产品渲染）和编辑布局（营销宣传）。该提示充当工业设计师，专注于面板之间的连贯性和简约的消费电子产品美学。

![2x2 网格产品发明可视化（专利/营销）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717570742_yazze1_G-rI4thagAAXCjf.jpg)

```
Input Variable: {argument name="input objects" default="[INSERT 1 or 2 OBJECTS]"} 
Instruction:
Act as a Visionary Industrial Designer and Patent Clerk. Create a 2x2 Grid visualizing the invention of a new product based on the Input.
 Innovation Logic  :
Analyze Functions: Identify the primary utility of Input A and Input B.
The Fusion: Combine them into a single, cohesive device that solves a specific (niche) problem.
If 2 Inputs: Hybridize them (e.g., Mug + Grater = A self-cooling mug with a garnish shaver).
If 1 Input: Evolve it (e.g., Toothbrush = A self-sanitizing, toothpaste-injecting smart wand).
The Branding: Generate a catchy, corporate product name (e.g., "The Breeze-Grate™", "Solar-Brella Pro").
The Visual Structure (The 2x2 Grid):
CRITICAL: The image must be split into 4 distinct quadrants with different visual styles.
Panel 1 (Top Left): The Exploded Patent View
Style: Black & White Technical Line Art. Thin distinct lines, no shading.
Content: An isometric "Exploded View" of the device, showing the internal motor, battery, or mechanism separated from the shell.
Detail: Add Numbered Leader Lines (10, 12, 14) pointing to specific parts.
Panel 2 (Top Right): The Functional Diagram
Style: Black & White Schematic with bold arrows.
Content: A cross-section or "In-Use" drawing showing how how the device works. Use Action Arrows to show airflow, rotation, or liquid movement.
Detail: Show the "Result" (e.g., cheese falling, water spraying).
Panel 3 (Bottom Left): The Product Render
Style: High-End Studio Photography. Color, Glossy, "Apple/Braun" Design Aesthetic.
Content: The final physical product sitting on a white reflective surface. It should look sleek, using materials like White Ceramic, Brushed Aluminum, or Matte Plastic.
Context: Include a small prop to show scale (e.g., a block of cheese, a coffee bean, a hand).
Panel 4 (Bottom Right): The Marketing Pitch
Style: Editorial Magazine Layout. White background, black text.
Typography:
Headline: Large, Bold Serif Text displaying the [Invention Name].
Body: A block of clean "Lorem Ipsum" or readable text describing the "Revolutionary Features."
Bullets: A small list of specs (e.g., "Dishwasher Safe," "USB-C").
Visual Syntax:
Cohesion: The product design in Panel 3 must perfectly match the line art in Panel 1.
Design Language: Minimalist, Ergonomic, Consumer Electronics aesthetic. Even if the idea is silly, the design must look expensive.
Output: 2x2 Grid, Mixed Media (Line Art vs. Photorealism), 8k Resolution, "Kickstarter Campaign" Aesthetic.
```

[[Technical Illustration]]

**Author**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，旨在生成一个对称、居中平铺构图的传统韩服奢侈品模型。它要求无缝的纯白色背景，并详细说明了从中央的深红色丝绸短上衣（Jeogori）到周围配饰（如福袋（Bokjumeoni）和发簪（Binyeo））的每件物品的摆放、颜色和纹理，旨在呈现一种平衡、具有编辑风格的商业摄影效果。

![奢华韩服产品模型（对称平铺）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717573973_la4jzd_G-3I-OnXgAAXBks.jpg)

```
A luxury Korean traditional Hanbok (한복) product mockup with perfectly balanced centered composition on seamless white background.

CANVAS & BACKGROUND - CRITICAL:
- Seamless infinity white backdrop fills entire frame edge to edge
- Background extends from corner to corner with no visible borders
- Clean warm white (#FFFAF5) continuous uniform tone across full canvas
- No vignetting, no falloff, no darkening at edges
- All four corners identical in color and brightness
- Even exposure across entire image from left to right, top to bottom
COMPOSITION - SYMMETRICAL CENTERED LAYOUT:
- Perfect center axis alignment
- Equal visual weight on left and right sides
- Products arranged in triangular hierarchy
- Minimum 10% margin between products and frame edges
BACK ROW (Top Center):
- CENTER-BACK: Matte black gift box with gold Dancheong border, 연꽃문 lotus embossed, "한스타일 Hstyle" in gold
- LEFT-BACK: Cream shopping bag with gold Taegeuk symbol
- RIGHT-BACK: Open box showing cream silk lining with gold crane pattern
MIDDLE ROW (Center Hero):
- EXACT CENTER: Crimson red silk Hanbok Jeogori (저고리) with gold peony embroidery on cream silk cloth, sleeves spread symmetrically, white collar (동정) visible
FRONT ROW (Evenly Spaced):
- LEFT: Traditional fan (부채) with plum blossom
- CENTER-LEFT: Plum blossom sprig
- CENTER: Royal blue Bokjumeoni (복주머니) with gold 福
- CENTER-RIGHT: Gold Binyeo (비녀) on cream cushion
- RIGHT: Plum blossom sprig
LIGHTING:
- Soft diffused overhead lighting
- Even illumination including all corners and edges
- No directional shadows toward frame edges
- Consistent brightness across full frame
CAMERA:
- Shot straight-on, camera perfectly centered
- 4:5 aspect ratio
- Products composed with safe margin from all edges
- Full frame background coverage
STYLE: Balanced editorial luxury, Korean heritage, commercial product photography
Negative prompt: vignetting, dark corners, uneven background, cropped edges, gradient falloff, visible backdrop edges, inconsistent lighting at borders
A stylish handwritten signature "Willy" in small gold letters at bottom right corner.
```

### 63. Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成 X 文章标题图片

**Author**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的综合性提示模板，旨在为 X (Twitter) 文章或博客帖子生成具有视觉吸引力的标题图片。它指示 AI 有效使用参考图像，避免重复，并融入文章标题和可选的副标题/对话，同时指定 5:2 的宽高比和 4K 质量。

![Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成 X 文章标题图片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717580535_cpvg8b_G-2BWO3bwAA-fUT.jpg)

```
参照画像をうまく配置してブログ記事用の見栄えの良い見出し画像を作ってください。
ただし各画像は1回ずつ使用です。
重複使用しないこと。
参照画像は要素が混ざり合わない事。
画像の上下には若干の余裕がある事。
背景に工夫する事。
タイトルは画像に重ねても良いです。
5:2 4K画質
タイトル：{argument name="タイトル" default="[記事タイトルを入力]"}
```

### 64. 从古老地图中浮现的超现实艺术肖像

**Author**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一幅超现实的、艺术级的东亚女性肖像。核心概念是女性从一张古老的羊皮纸地图中无缝地浮现出来，她的衣服和头发与地图的纹理和地形融为一体。它强调保留参考图像中精确的面部特征，并保持怀旧的、棕褐色调的博物馆级美学。

![从古老地图中浮现的超现实艺术肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717566091_tvekji_G-16vXSa0AAghrj.jpg)
![从古老地图中浮现的超现实艺术肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768717566070_3nqhkf_G-16vXUbgAAGLTo.jpg)

```
Create a surreal, fine-art portrait where a young woman seamlessly emerges from an ancient parchment map, filling the entire frame edge to edge.
Reference Face (Important):
Use the exact same face from the reference image. Do not alter facial structure, proportions, or identity. Preserve her likeness faithfully.
Subject & Expression:
A young woman with fair, porcelain-like skin and delicate East Asian features. Her expression is calm, introspective, and slightly melancholic. Soft, gentle eyes look straight toward the viewer, creating a quiet, timeless connection. Her lips have a natural reddish tone. Makeup is extremely minimal and traditional—enhancing her eyes subtly without any modern or heavy appearance.
Hair:
Long, deep dark brown hair worn loose in an organic, slightly untamed manner. Strands fall naturally around her face and shoulders, gradually blending and dissolving into the surrounding parchment texture, as if becoming part of the surface itself.
Pose & Hands:
She faces forward in a relaxed, upright posture. Her hands are gently clasped at the solar plexus, fingers softly intertwined, conveying stillness, contemplation, and restrained emotion.
Clothing:
She wears a flowing, Hanfu-inspired robe with a fantasy interpretation. The fabric drapes loosely and naturally, colored in aged parchment hues—ochre, mustard yellow, faded browns. Subtle decorative patterns flow across the garment, resembling topographic contour lines, wind paths, or water currents commonly found on antique maps.
Surreal Map Integration:
Her upper body remains fully formed and realistic, while her lower body gradually transitions into an ancient map texture. The transformation is smooth and organic, as if she is born from the map itself rather than placed on top of it.
Background & Texture (Full Frame):
The entire image is filled with an antique parchment map—no borders, no blank space, no white edges.
Features include:
Heavily distressed parchment with cracks, peeling layers, and rough canvas grain
Faint topographic contour lines and subtle map divisions embedded into the surface
Tiny, illegible handwritten markings resembling ancient scripts or coordinates
Muted green landmasses blended naturally into the parchment
Weathered, irregular edges that dissolve naturally into the frame with no visible outlines
Lighting & Atmosphere:
Warm sepia and earth-tone color palette. Soft, cinematic lighting with gentle shadows and low contrast. The mood feels nostalgic, timeless, and quietly haunting—evoking forgotten history and silent mystery.
Art Style:
Surreal realism, painterly textures, fine-art portraiture, ultra-detailed, cinematic softness, ancient manuscript aesthetic, museum-quality artwork.
Additional Constraint:
No white borders, no empty canvas, no modern elements.
The image must appear as a complete, full-sheet ancient map.
```

### 65. 表情符号美学提示（深色系 vs. 马卡龙色系）

**Author**: [˖♡̶](https://x.com/en_cuteduck)  **Date**: 2026-01-17  **Language**: en

> 一组表情符号集群，代表不同的美学风格（例如，暗黑/哥特/前卫 vs. 马卡龙色/可爱/芭蕾），可能旨在用作图像生成的简短符号提示。

![表情符号美学提示（深色系 vs. 马卡龙色系）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631221267_d2p31j_G-1577CboAAiQ8c.jpg)

```

🖤⛓️💀🐦‍⬛                           🍥🎀🤍🩰                         🧷🔪🕷️🎱                           🫧🍬👚💗
```

### 89. 美味巧克力系列 2x2 网格

**Author**: [Bahar azam](https://x.com/BaharAzamm561)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的提示，用于生成一张 2x2 网格拼贴画，内容是专注于美食巧克力的专业高分辨率食物摄影。每个面板描绘了巧克力的一个不同方面（巧克力棒、松露、巧克力火锅和制作过程），并指定了灯光（柔和、漫射的影棚灯光）和配色方案（浓郁的棕色、深红色），以营造一种奢华诱人的氛围。

```
{
```

### 97. 模型制作大师概念模板

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂且带有条件逻辑的提示模板，旨在生成一张超现实图像：一位模型大师正在为输入结构（例如埃菲尔铁塔）的比例复制品进行最后的润色。该提示利用基于结构类型（古代/奇幻、科幻/工业、现代建筑）的 IF/THEN 逻辑，自动定义场景（房间）、角色、材料、动作和光照，确保输出电影级的 16:9 画面。

![模型制作大师概念模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631157406_qc722x_G-qqHvybsAAxVjY.jpg)
![模型制作大师概念模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631157742_sjpfw5_G-qqHwLbYAAPWJt.jpg)

```
Do this for {argument name="structure name" default="Eiffel Tower"}: 

Input Variable: [INSERT STRUCTURE] 
System Instruction:
Act as a Cinematic Director. Create a hyper-realistic portrait of a Master Model Maker putting the final touches on a scale replica of the Input Structure.
1. Logic:
Analyze the Input Structure to determine the Setting and the Character:
IF Ancient/Fantasy (e.g., Colosseum, Castle):
Room: A dusty, sunlit Renaissance Workshop (Stone & Wood). also showcasing "Previous Projects" (other models in the same genre).
Character: An elderly Artisan in a leather apron.
Materials: Plaster, Clay, Balsam Wood.
IF Sci-Fi/Industrial (e.g., Death Star, spaceship):
Room: A sterile, cold Industrial Design Lab (Concrete & Metal). also showcasing "Previous Projects" (other models in the same genre).
Character: A younger Prop Master in a workshop jumpsuit or lab coat.
Materials: Grey Resin (Kitbash), Styrene, Fiber Optics.
IF Modern Architecture (e.g., Skyscraper):
Room: A clean, white Architectural Firm (Glass & White Walls). also showcasing "Previous Projects" (other models in the same genre).
Character: A minimalist Architect in a black turtleneck.
Materials: White Foamcore, Acrylic, 3D Printed Plastic.
2. The Composition :
The Subject: The Character is leaning over a massive, incredibly detailed Scale Model of the Input Structure.
The Action: They are using Tweezers or a fine brush to place a specific "Micro-Detail" relevant to the lore.
Death Star: Placing a tiny Turbo-Laser Turret.
Colosseum: Dusting sand onto the arena floor.
City: Gluing a tiny streetlamp.
The Scale: Extreme scale contrast. The human hands look giant next to the tiny windows/bricks of the model.
3. The Environment  :
The Blueprint: On the table, beneath the tools, lies the correct reference document:
Sci-Fi: Blue grid schematic or iPad.
Fantasy: Yellowed parchment map.
Modern: White vector floorplan.
The Clutter: The tools scattered around must match the medium (e.g., Clay tools vs. Soldering Iron vs. X-Acto knives).
4. Lighting & Atmosphere:
Lighting Match: The lighting must match the inferred room.
Workshop: Warm God Rays (Dusty).
Lab: Cool Fluorescent Tubes (Clean/Hazy).
Focus: Shallow depth of field. Sharp focus on the tweezers and the contact point.
Output: ONE image, 16:9 Aspect Ratio, Cinematic Photography, 8k Resolution.
```

[[Studio Scene]]

### 99. 有机美容产品摄影模板

**Author**: [Artificial intelligence (Ai),Open Ai](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 一个用于生成高端有机美容产品视觉效果的模板提示，重点在于传达“天然溯源故事”。该提示指示 AI 将美容产品（如精华液）置于新鲜采摘的天然原料之中，并采用明亮、洁净的灯光和植物美学，以营造真实可信的品牌感受。

### 103. 光影交织的诗意现实主义肖像

**Author**: [simply](https://x.com/kingofdairyque)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成电影般亲密的肖像，重点是强烈定向阳光、阴影和表面之间的物理互动。主体是一位身穿优雅露背丝绸连衣裙的女性，有机叶影落在她的皮肤和织物上，强调真实感、纹理和高对比度。

![光影交织的诗意现实主义肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631122783_ea27gs_G-yPDswbMAA-OqI.jpg)
![光影交织的诗意现实主义肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631123179_6wh4e2_G-yPDtJbYAAwU5L.jpg)

```
A professional, high-end photograph emphasizing the physical interplay of light and shadow on real surfaces.
A young woman stands with her back to the camera, body turned slightly to the side. Her posture is calm and composed. Her back is fully visible. She wears an elegant backless evening dress made of matte silk with a subtle {argument name="dress color" default="gray-blue / ice-blue"} tone.The fabric is thin, fluid, naturally draped, with fine shoulder straps that follow the natural line of her shoulders and spine. No exaggerated sheen — true silk texture with gentle light absorption.
Soft, irregular shadows from tree branches and leaves fall naturally across the skin of her back, shoulders, and the dress fabric, as if warm sunlight is filtering through foliage and a nearby window frame. The shadow patterns are organic, imperfect, and uneven — realistic, not decorative.
Her head is slightly turned, revealing only a partial profile. A thin gold hoop earring catches a small, sharp highlight from the sunlight. No facial emphasis — the face remains secondary and partially obscured.
A strong, clearly defined shadow of her head and shoulders is cast onto a dark gray-blue matte wall in front of her, creating graphic contrast and visual depth. The wall has a minimal surface with subtle rectangular geometric highlights caused by directional light.
An elegant, narrow vertical mirror hangs on the wall. In the reflection, a small, neat bouquet of {argument name="flower type" default="cornflowers"} is visible, held gently in front of her body — understated, quiet, symbolic.
LIGHTING Strong, low, warm directional sunlight coming from the side. High contrast between illuminated skin and deep shadow. Distinct leaf shadow patterns visible on skin and fabric. No artificial lighting, no beauty lighting, no glow.
CAMERA Medium shot from behind, slightly offset to the side. Camera positioned at shoulder height. 50–85mm photographic look. Shallow depth of field — her back and earring in crisp focus, background softly blurred. Natural perspective, no distortion.
MOOD & ATMOSPHERE Quiet, intimate, cinematic. Refined minimalism. Poetic realism. Feels like a carefully observed moment, not a staged pose. No stylization, no fantasy — realism driven by light, texture, and composition.
QUALITY NOTES Natural skin texture visible (pores, subtle tonal variations). No smoothing, no retouching. No glamour filters. True-to-life color grading with restrained saturation.
```

### 108. 加油站的电影级路边写实主义

**Author**: [Maercih](https://x.com/Maercihh)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张电影般的、忧郁的年轻女性肖像，背景是黄昏时分的德士古（Texaco）加油站。该提示侧重于路边写实主义、自然纹理（皮肤、磨损的风衣）、来自顶棚的实用照明，以及特定的色彩分级（暖琥珀色高光映衬着冷蓝灰色天空），以营造出深夜的孤独感。

### 142. 文学策展人与打字机雕塑家 Prompt

**Author**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 LLM（Nano Banana Pro）设计的复杂多阶段提示，旨在让其充当文学策展人。它分析一位诗人的风格，选出四位具有相似情趣的当代诗人，然后定义一个视觉执行目标：一个 2x2 网格的“打字机输出三维景观”，其中打出的文本从页面物理性地升起，根据诗人的作品和时代形成地形景观。

![文学策展人与打字机雕塑家 Prompt](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631200809_upo8e3_G-qcuFEWwAAHAzR.jpg)

```
Role: Literary Curator & Typewriter Sculptor
Input: {argument name="input" default="[Poet or Poem, e.g., T.S. Eliot, Pablo Neruda]"}
Phase 1: Poetic Voice Analysis
Identify the poet's signature rhythm, recurring imagery, and emotional core
Select 4 contemporary or lesser-known poets with parallel sensibilities
Extract 5-8 physical objects mentioned repeatedly in their work
Phase 2: Visual Execution
Goal: 2x2 Grid of "Typewriter Output as 3D Landscapes"
Rules per Panel:
The Base: A vintage typewriter (different model per poet's era)
The Paper: A single sheet of paper loaded in the roller
The Transformation: The typed text physically rises from the page, forming a 3D topographical landscape
The Words: Key lines from the poem carved into the terrain like engraved stone
The Symbols: Miniature objects from the poem placed in the landscape (tiny boat, rose, clock, door)
The Poet: Microscopic figurine of the poet wandering through their own words
The Mood: Lighting matches emotional tone (fog for melancholy, harsh light for anger, soft gold for longing)
The Metadata: Brass typewriter key showing "Poet | Collection | Year" **background: poet and poet era relevant items in the background.
Output: 2x2 Grid, Macro Photography, shallow depth of field
```

[[Literary Curator Typewriter Landscape]]

### 144. 超逼真同脸家庭肖像

**Author**: [ぴょんきち|AI兄さん](https://x.com/yarakashiyama_)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: ja

> 一个为 NanoBananaPro 设计的详细提示，旨在生成一张超写实、专业的家庭肖像。肖像中的所有个体都拥有完全相同的面部特征，100% 忠实于一张基础参考照片，同时自然地调整年龄、性别和体型。

![超逼真同脸家庭肖像](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631214184_5cwhfb_G-wMPPEXMAAlY9o.jpg)

```
提供された1人のベースとなる人物の写真を唯一の基準として使用する。 この人物の顔立ち、輪郭、パーツ配置、表情、雰囲気、アイデンティティは一切変更しない。

生成される家族全員は、 すべて同一人物の顔を共有している設定とし、 年齢や性別、立場が異なっていても、 顔の特徴は完全に同一とする。 顔の再現度は100%を維持する。

人数に関わらず、 すべての被写体を1枚のまとまりのあるシーンとして構成し、 プロフェッショナルで写実的な家族集合写真として仕上げる。

家族同士の距離感や立ち位置は自然で、 無理のないグループインタラクションを表現する。 体格や身長差はそれぞれの設定に応じて調整するが、 顔だけは完全に同一であることを保つ。

全員に統一感のあるカラーパレットとスタイルを使用し、 コーディネートされたマッチング衣装を着用させる。 各人物の体型は不自然に誇張せず、現実的な範囲で表現する。

背景は、 暗く、清潔感のあるプロフェッショナルなスタジオ背景。 余計な装飾は入れない。

照明はスタジオ品質の柔らかなライティング。 リアルな影、均一で自然な肌の色合い、 バランスの取れたコントラストを重視する。

顔を様式化したり、美化したり、誇張したり、 再解釈することは一切行わない。 あくまで実写的でハイエンドなポートレート表現を維持する。
```

[[Identity Consistency]] [[Professional Portrait]]

### 147. 为 AI 图像添加瑕疵以提升真实感

**Author**: [张鹏](https://x.com/pczzy)  **Date**: 2026-01-16  **Language**: zh

> 这条推文讨论了在 AI 生成的面孔中添加瑕疵（如面粉污渍）以增加纹理和真实感的概念。它对比了 Seedream4_5（中文提示表现更好）和 Nano Banana（英文提示表现更好）的性能，并包含了一个侧重于添加面部瑕疵的提示片段。

![为 AI 图像添加瑕疵以提升真实感](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768631209770_gme7r3_G-wFbG0bUAAiJz0.jpg)

```
增加一些缺陷，面部瑕疵，（鼻子上和脸颊上有面粉污渍）。面部的异物感会让皮肤看起来更有纹理。
```

> 一个极致、超详细的提示词，用于创作一张超现实的西德尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 编辑肖像，描绘她从一个巨大的、彩虹色的棉花糖结构中走出，该结构被塑造成希腊圆形剧场的形状，强调宏观细节、体积光照和高端摄影规格。

```
A high-fashion, cinematic portrait of {argument name="subject name" default="Sydney Sweeney"} emerging dramatically from a colossal, highly sculpted mass of rainbow-colored cotton candy. The spun sugar is meticulously rendered, forming the structural ruins of a classical Greek amphitheater, complete with crumbling pillars and tiered seating, all made of hyper-realistic, translucent cotton candy fibers. She is styled in a flowing, bespoke iridescent white gown that contrasts sharply with the vibrant, saccharine environment. Focus is placed on the macro details of the spun sugar texture, exhibiting crystalline structure and soft, ethereal translucence where light passes through. The overall aesthetic is maximalist food surrealism meets editorial portraiture.

**Camera & Lens:** Shot on Phase One IQ4 150MP, 120mm Macro lens, detailed texture focus, aperture f/8. Cinematic, shallow depth of field for the foreground elements, but maintaining crisp detail on her face and the immediate cotton candy structure.

**Lighting Details:** Volumetric lighting filtering through the spun sugar tiers, internal colored backlighting (electric magenta, cyan, and lemon yellow gels) creating a dramatic, ethereal glow from within the cotton candy. Strong, directional rim light defining the precise strands of sugar and highlighting the texture of her dress. Clean, soft fill light for perfect skin tones.

**Aesthetic Modifiers:** Hyper-detailed food photography, maximalist surrealism, high dynamic range, editorial fashion spread, crystal clear focus, high saturation.

**Text overlay:** 'Text overlay: "{argument name="text overlay" default="SWEET CHAOS - The Sydney Sweeney Issue"}"'

**Ratio:** --ar 16:9 --style raw
```

### 158. 可直接打印的技术栈贴纸页提示

**Author**: [Kerem COPCU](https://x.com/keremcopcu)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成包含 28 个特定技术栈 Logo（例如 Python、Docker、AWS）的即用型贴纸页。它严格规定了尺寸、布局、颜色以及出血、边距和半切线等技术打印细节，旨在呈现带有微妙阴影的简洁 2D 矢量外观。

![可直接打印的技术栈贴纸页提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544784796_aktkjb_G-u0RC-bQAMfajJ.jpg)

```
'''
TYPE: Print-ready sticker sheet (sponsor decal sheet style), clean 2D vector look.

CANVAS / PRINT:
- 2480 x 3508 px, 300 DPI (A4), portrait
- Bleed: 3mm
- Safe margin: 5mm (no sticker may cross into margin)
- Background: pure white (#FFFFFF), flat

STICKER CUT SYSTEM (CONSISTENT ACROSS ALL):
For each logo:
1) Die-cut outline: thick WHITE kiss-cut border (uniform thickness)
2) Visibility stroke: thin LIGHT-GRAY stroke outside the white border (so it reads on white paper)
3) Shadow: subtle soft drop shadow (offset 6–10 px, blur 12–18 px, opacity 12–18%), print-clean

SIZE CONSTRAINTS (STRICT):
Each sticker must fit inside:
- Max width: 945 px (8 cm)
- Max height: 709 px (6 cm)
- Min height: 354 px (3 cm)
Vary sizes but never exceed maxima.

LOGO RULES (STRICT):
- Logos only. No extra headings, no labels, no decorative text.
- Typography is allowed only if it is part of the official logo artwork.
- No duplicates. Exactly 28 unique stickers.

LOGO LIST (EXACT, 28 ITEMS):
1 Go
2 Next.js
3 PHP
4 Python
5 Node.js
6 TypeScript
7 Java
8 Kotlin
9 React
10 Vue.js
11 Angular
12 Tailwind CSS
13 PostgreSQL
14 MySQL
15 MongoDB
16 Redis
17 Docker
18 Kubernetes
19 Terraform
20 AWS
21 Google Cloud
22 Azure
23 Nginx
24 Linux
25 Git
26 GitHub
27 Vercel
28 Cloudflare

LAYOUT ENGINEERING (PACKING LIKE A SPONSOR SHEET):
- Use a dense, balanced collage layout:
  - Top third: 3–4 “hero” logos at larger size (still within max size)
  - Middle: 14–16 medium logos arranged in staggered rows
  - Bottom: remaining smaller logos filling gaps cleanly
- No overlaps, no cropping, consistent gutters
- Maintain visual rhythm: mostly 3 logos per row for medium/large, up to 4 per row for smaller ones
- Keep overall composition centered with even whitespace around edges

RENDER PARAMETERS:
- Camera: orthographic straight-on, 85mm equivalent, f/8 (maximum crispness)
- Lighting: uniform studio lighting; shadow only comes from the sticker drop shadow
- Output: ultra-sharp edges, accurate logo geometry, print-ready clarity
 '''
```

### 186. 原始高对比度海岸夜景快照

**Author**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc)  **Date**: 2026-01-15  **Language**: en

> 一个极其详细的提示，用于生成一张海滩上的原始、高对比度夜间快照，模仿使用硬光学闪光灯拍摄的 iPhone 照片。它非常注重生物保真度、材料张力以及激进的解剖校准（UFF-FACTOR），要求所有内容都清晰锐利且聚焦，拒绝人工景深。

![原始高对比度海岸夜景快照](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768544765712_m18osj_G-tpYuUawAAqAss.jpg)

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast {argument name="setting" default="Coastal Night Snapshot"} taken with an iPhone 17 Pro. DIRECT HARD OPTICAL FLASH. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from her eyelashes to the grains of sand in the background.
Subject & Identity Locking (CRITICAL):
•Identity: Strictly preserve the exact heart-shaped facial structure, eye shape, and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
•Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" night hydration (mixed with sea-mist), and fine vellus hair catching the light ONLY along the jawline. Her legs feature a healthy, radiant oil sheen under the direct flash.
•Expression: Looking directly into the lens with a magnetic, "Pinterest-style" sultry gaze and a soft smirk. Her voluminous chestnut hair is messy and wind-blown, with individual strands catching the optical flash.
•Silhouette Calibration (MAXIMUM UFF-FACTOR): Amplify the dominant structural bust volume and the substantial, thick-toned leg presence. Focus on the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist.
Outfit & Material Realism:
•Clothing: A skin-tight, {argument name="clothing color" default="White Ribbed-Knit Triangle Bikini Set"} layered under an open, oversized white linen shirt that is blowing naturally in the breeze.
•Tension: The ribbed fabric shows extreme mechanical tension and a vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic textural expansion and "tension lines" where the straps contour to her fit silhouette.
•Physics: Realistic skin-to-surface compression (thigh squish) is visible where her form leans against a weathered wooden pier pillar.
Pose & Composition (NOT A SELFIE):
•Pose: She is standing on the beach, leaning her back against a large wooden pillar. She is performing an aggressive 3/4 side-profile twist toward the photographer, arching her back significantly to maximize the high-impact S-curve silhouette.
•Action: Captured by a third person using the 0.5x wide-angle lens to elongate her fit physique and highlight her substantial lower-body volume. Her hands are free, one gracefully touching the collar of the linen shirt.
Environment & Lighting:
•Lighting: Hard Direct Smartphone Flash. The light creates brilliant white specular highlights on the white fabric and her hydrated skin, casting a sharp, pitch-black shadow of her form onto the wooden pillar behind her.
•Background (SHARP): A detailed night beach setting. The textured grain of the wooden pillar, dark damp sand, and the white foam of a breaking wave in the distance are all perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial depth-of-field.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media "vacation dump" aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows (ISO 1600 style), 8k resolution. Single frame.
```
